# <a name="dimensions-and-measurements-available-in-call-quality-dashboard"></a><span data-ttu-id="61209-103">[通話品質] 儀表板中提供的尺寸與測量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-103">Dimensions and measurements available in Call Quality Dashboard</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="61209-104">Microsoft 團隊和商務用 Skype Online 的通話品質儀表板（CQD）可讓您更清楚地瞭解使用這些服務進行通話的通話品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-104">The Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online allows you to better understand call quality of calls made with these services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-105">本主題提供透過 CQD 顯示之維度與度量的詳細資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-105">This topic provides detailed information about the dimensions and measurements visible through CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-106">若要深入瞭解 CQD，請參閱[開啟與使用 Microsoft 團隊和商務用 Skype Online 的通話品質儀表板](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-106">To learn more about CQD, see [Turning on and using Call Quality Dashboard for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>

## <a name="first-and-second-endpoint-classification"></a><span data-ttu-id="61209-107">第一和第二個端點分類</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-107">First and Second endpoint classification</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="61209-108">CQD 中的許多尺寸與測量值標示為第一或第二筆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-108">Many of the dimensions and measurements in CQD are labeled as first or second.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-109">下列邏輯會判斷資料流程或呼叫中所涉及的端點標示為「第一」：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-109">The following logic determines which endpoint involved in the stream or call is labeled as first:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="61209-110">伺服器端點（AV MCU、中繼伺服器等）是在資料流程或通話中參與伺服器時，最先考慮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-110">A Server endpoint (AV MCU, Mediation Server, and so on) is considered First when a Server is involved in the stream or call.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="61209-111">除非資料流程位於兩個伺服器端點之間，否則會視為第二個用戶端端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-111">A Client endpoint is considered Second unless the stream is between two Server endpoints.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="61209-112">如果兩個端點都是相同的類型，則會根據使用者代理類別的內部排序來設定，以確保順序一致。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-112">If both endpoints are the same type, first vs. second is set based on internal ordering of the user agent category to ensure that the ordering is consistent.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="61209-113">例如，以下每個資料列代表一個串流中所涉及的一對使用者代理程式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-113">For example, here each row represents a pair of User Agents involved in a stream:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="61209-114">來電者的使用者代理類別</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-114">User Agent Category of Caller</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-115">被呼叫者的使用者代理類別</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-115">User Agent Category of Callee</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-116">第一個端點</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-116">First Endpoint</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-117">第二個端點</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-117">Second Endpoint</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="61209-118">首先是來電者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-118">First Is Caller</span></span>
|:--- |:--- |:--- |:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-119">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-119">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-120">OC （商務用 Skype 用戶端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-120">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-121">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-121">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-122">OC （商務用 Skype 用戶端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-122">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-123">滿足</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-123">TRUE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-124">OC （商務用 Skype 用戶端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-124">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-125">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-125">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-126">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-126">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-127">OC （商務用 Skype 用戶端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-127">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-128">虛假</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-128">FALSE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-129">OC （商務用 Skype 用戶端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-129">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-130">OC （商務用 Skype 用戶端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-130">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-131">OC （商務用 Skype 用戶端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-131">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-132">OC （商務用 Skype 用戶端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-132">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-133">虛假</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-133">FALSE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-134">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-134">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-135">中繼伺服器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-135">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-136">中繼伺服器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-136">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-137">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-137">AV-MCU</span></span> ||
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-138">中繼伺服器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-138">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-139">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-139">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-140">中繼伺服器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-140">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-141">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-141">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-142">滿足</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-142">TRUE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-143">OC （商務用 Skype 用戶端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-143">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-144">OC 電話（商務用 Skype IP 電話）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-144">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-145">OC （商務用 Skype 用戶端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-145">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-146">OC 電話（商務用 Skype IP 電話）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-146">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-147">滿足</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-147">TRUE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-148">OC 電話（商務用 Skype IP 電話）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-148">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-149">OC （商務用 Skype 用戶端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-149">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-150">OC （商務用 Skype 用戶端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-150">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-151">OC 電話（商務用 Skype IP 電話）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-151">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-152">虛假</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-152">FALSE</span></span> |

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="61209-153">第一和第二種分類是獨立于來電者或被叫商的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-153">That First and Second classification is separate from which endpoint is the caller or callee.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-154">第一個是呼叫方維度可用來協助找出哪個端點是呼叫者或被叫方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-154">The First Is Caller dimension can be used to help identify which endpoint was the caller or callee.</span></span>

## <a name="dimensions"></a><span data-ttu-id="61209-155">三維</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-155">Dimensions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="61209-156">維度資訊是根據上傳到 CQD 入口網站的資料而定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-156">Dimensions information is based in part on data uploaded to the CQD portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-157">許多維度值也可以用來做為篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-157">Many Dimension values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-158">下表列出目前在 CQD 中可用的維度，按照用來建立報表或編輯先前定義的報表的 [查詢編輯器] 中所列的順序進行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-158">The following table lists the dimensions currently available in CQD, in the order listed in the Query Editor used to create reports or edit previously defined reports.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="61209-159">名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-159">Name</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-160">資料類型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-160">Data type</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="61209-161">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-161">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-162">空白值的可能原因</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-162">Possible Reasons for blank values</span></span> |
|:---  |:---        |:---         |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-163">**端點**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-163">**Endpoint**</span></span>|||
| <span data-ttu-id="61209-164">第一個 CPU 名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-164">First CPU Name</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="61209-165">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-165">String</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="61209-166">第一個端點所使用之 CPU 的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-166">Name of the CPU used by the first endpoint.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="61209-167">**範例值：** Contoso CPU X11 @ 1.80 GHz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-167">**Example value:** Contoso CPU X11 @ 1.80 GHz</span></span> | <br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-168">&bull;端點未報告此資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-168">&bull; This data was not reported by the endpoint</span></span>   |

data-ttu-id="61209-2442">使用者 > 通話方案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2442">user -> calling plan</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2443">byot-> 直接路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2443">byot -> direct routing</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2444">會議 > 音訊會議</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2444">conf -> audio conferencing</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2445">ucap-> 語音應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2445">ucap -> voice app</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2446">緊急 > 緊急號碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2446">emergency -> emergency number</span></span><br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2447">撥號類型：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2447">Call type:</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2448">> 撥入通話</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2448">In -> inbound call</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2449">外 > 輸出通話</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2449">Out -> outbound call</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2450">Out_transfer > 向外通話轉移給第三人</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2450">Out_transfer -> outbound call gets transferred to third person</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2451">Out_forward > 撥出電話轉接給第三人</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2451">Out_forward -> outbound call gets forwarded to third person</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2452">使用點對點 PSTN 參與者 Out_conf > 出站通話</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2452">Out_conf ->  outbound call with ad-hoc PSTN participant</span></span><br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2453">**範例：** ByotIn</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2453">**Example:** ByotIn</span></span>||
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2454">PSTN 連線類型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2454">PSTN Connectivity Type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2455">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2455">String</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2456">PSTN 連線類型包括直接路由、通話方案或音訊會議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2456">PSTN connectivity type includes Direct Routing, Calling Plan, or Audio Conferencing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-2457">目前，通話品質儀表板（CQD）只提供直接路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2457">At this time, only Direct Routing is available in the Call Quality Dashboard (CQD).</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2458">**範例：** 直接路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2458">**Example:** Direct Routing</span></span>||

|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2463">PSTN 通話結束 Sub 原因</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2463">PSTN Call End Sub Reason</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2464">Int</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2464">Int</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2465">從 Microsoft 元件發出的回應代碼，指出發生的特定動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2465">A response code sent out from the Microsoft component that indicates specific actions that occurred.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2466">**範例：** 540000</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2466">**Example:** 540000</span></span>||
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2467">PSTN 事件種類</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2467">PSTN Event Type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2468">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2468">String</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2469">提供遙測的事件種類。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2469">An event type that provides telemetry.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2470">**範例：** 處</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2470">**Example:** End</span></span>||
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2471">PSTN 事件資訊時間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2471">PSTN Event Info Time</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2472">為止</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2472">Date</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2473">從 Microsoft 網路開始撥出電話或撥入通話到達 Microsoft 網路時，以 UTC 格式表示的時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2473">The time in UTC format when an outbound call starts from the Microsoft network or an inbound call reaches the Microsoft network.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2474">**範例：** 2020-02-06 20：57：53.1750000</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2474">**Example:** 2020-02-06 20:57:53.1750000</span></span>||
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2475">PSTN MP 位置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2475">PSTN MP Location</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2476">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2476">String</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2477">在非旁路模式下，媒體處理器位置會顯示媒體路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2477">The Media Processor location will show the media path when in non-bypass mode.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2478">**範例：** USWE</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2478">**Example:** USWE</span></span>||
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2479">第一個 PSTN 國家地區</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2479">First PSTN Country Region</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2480">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2480">String</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2481">如果 FirstIsCaller 為 true，則第一個 PSTN 國家地區就是來電者的國家/地區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2481">If FirstIsCaller is true, First PSTN Country Region is the caller's country.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-2482">如果是 false，則第二個 PSTN 國家/地區就是來電者的國家/地區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2482">If it is false, then Second PSTN Country region is the caller's country.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2483">**範例：** 一下</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2483">**Example:** US</span></span>||
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2484">抖動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2484">Jitter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2485">時間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2485">Milliseconds</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2486">RTP 資料包在到達時間內的變化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2486">The variation in arrival time of RTP packets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-2487">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[通話品質儀表板中的資料流程分類](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2487">Please see [Stream Classification in Call Quality Dashboard](stream-classification-in-call-quality-dashboard.md) for more information.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-2488">**範例：** 5.982</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2488">**Example:** 5.982</span></span>||

||||

### <a name="notes-on-dimension-data-typeunits"></a><span data-ttu-id="61209-2499">[維度] 資料類型/單位的備忘稿</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2499">Notes on dimension data type/units</span></span>

#### <a name="boolean"></a><span data-ttu-id="61209-2500">Boolean</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2500">Boolean</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="61209-2501">布林值通常是 True 或 False。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2501">Boolean values are always either True or False.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-2502">在某些情況下，True 也可以表示為1，而 False 則可以表示為0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2502">In some cases, True can also be represented as 1 and False can be represented as 0.</span></span>

#### <a name="range"></a><span data-ttu-id="61209-2503">大量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2503">Range</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="61209-2504">以下列格式顯示以範圍或值群組形式提供的尺寸：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2504">Dimensions that are provided as range or group of values are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="61209-2505">_\<排序次序字串\> [\<下限全形\> - \<（含上限）排他\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2505">_\<sort order string\> [\<lower bound inclusive\> - \<upper bound exclusive\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="61209-2506">例如，[工期] （分鐘）維度代表以秒為單位的值，以值為範圍來表示通話持續時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2506">For example, the Duration (Minutes) dimension represents the call duration in seconds with the value reported as a range of values.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2507">持續時間（分鐘）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2507">Duration (Minutes)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-2508">如何解讀</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2508">How to interpret</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2509">062： [0-0）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2509">062: [0 - 0)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-2510">資料流程持續時間 = 0 分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2510">Stream duration = 0 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2511">064： [1-2）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2511">064: [1 - 2)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-2512">1分鐘 < = 串流持續時間 < 2 分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2512">1 minute < = stream duration < 2 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2513">065： [2-3）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2513">065: [2 - 3)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-2514">2分鐘 < = 資料流程持續時間 < 3 分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2514">2 minutes < = stream duration < 3 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2515">066： [3 – 4]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2515">066: [3–4)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-2516">3分鐘 < = 資料流程持續時間 < 4 分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2516">3 minutes < = stream duration < 4 minutes</span></span> |
|  | |

<span data-ttu-id="61209-2517">\<排序次序字串> 用於在呈現資料時控制排序次序，並可用於篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2517">The \<sort order string> is used to control the sort order when presenting the data and can be used for filtering.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-2518">例如，[持續時間（分鐘）] < "065" 的篩選，會顯示持續時間少於2分鐘的資料流程（需要使用前導 "0" 才能如期作業）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2518">For example, a filter on Duration (Minutes) < "065", would show streams with duration less than 2 minutes (The leading '0' is needed for the filter to work as expected).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="61209-2519">排序次序字串的實際值並不重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2519">The actual value of the sort order string isn't significant.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-strings"></a><span data-ttu-id="61209-2520">列舉字串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2520">Enumeration strings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="61209-2521">CQD 所使用的字串通常是從資料檔案衍生而來，而且這些字元幾乎是在允許長度內的任何字元組合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2521">Strings used by CQD are often derived from data files, and these can be nearly any combination of character within the allowed length.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-2522">某些尺寸看起來像是字串，但由於它們只能是預先定義值的簡短清單中的其中一個，因此它們是列舉而不是 true 字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2522">Some dimensions look like strings, but since they can only be one of a short list of predefined values, they are enumerations and not true strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-2523">某些列舉字串也會成對使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2523">Some enumerations strings are also used in pairs.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-pair"></a><span data-ttu-id="61209-2524">列舉對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2524">Enumeration pair</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="61209-2525">以 [列舉] 對提供的尺寸會以下列格式顯示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2525">Dimensions that are provided as an enumeration pair are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="61209-2526">_\<從某個終點開始列舉值\> ： \<從其他端點的列舉值\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2526">_\<enumeration value from one end point\> : \<enumeration value from the other endpoint\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="61209-2527">列舉值的排序是一致的，但不會反映第一個或第二個端點的排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2527">The ordering of the enumeration values is consistent but doesn't reflect ordering of the first or second endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="61209-2528">例如，網路連線詳細資料對會顯示兩個端點的網路連線詳細值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2528">For example, the Network Connection Detail Pair shows the Network Connection Detail values for the two endpoints:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2529">網路連線詳細資料對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2529">Network Connection Detail Pair</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-2530">如何解讀</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2530">How to interpret</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2531">有線：有線</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2531">Wired : Wired</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-2532">第一和第二個端點都使用有線乙太網連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2532">First and second endpoints both used wired ethernet connections.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2533">有線： wifi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2533">Wired : wifi</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-2534">第一個端點使用有線乙太網連線和第二個端點使用 Wi-fi 連線，或第二個端點使用的是有線乙太網連線，而第二個端點使用 Wi-fi 連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2534">First endpoint used wired ethernet connection and second endpoint used Wi-Fi connection, or the second endpoint used wired ethernet connection and first endpoint used Wi-Fi connection.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-2535">： wifi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2535">: wifi</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="61209-2536">第一個端點使用 WiFi 連線，而第二個端點所使用的網路連線是未知的，或第二個端點使用 WiFi 連線，而第一個端點所使用的網路連線是未知的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2536">First endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the second endpoint is unknown, or the second endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the first endpoint is unknown.</span></span> |
| | |

#### <a name="blank-values"></a><span data-ttu-id="61209-2537">空白值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2537">Blank values</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="61209-2538">上表列出維度可能為空白的可能原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2538">The table above lists possible reasons why a dimension may be blank.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-2539">如果 QoE 記錄可用維度為 false，則許多維度和度量將會是空白的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2539">Many dimensions and measurements will be blank if the QoE Record Available dimension is false.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-2540">這通常是在通話未成功建立時發生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2540">This typically occurs when the call wasn't successfully established.</span></span>

## <a name="measurements"></a><span data-ttu-id="61209-2541">尺寸</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2541">Measurements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="61209-2542">許多測量值也可以用來做為篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2542">Many Measurement values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-2543">下表列出 CQD 中目前可用的度量，依 [查詢編輯器] 中列出的順序顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-2543">The following table lists the measurements currently available in CQD, shown in the order listed in the Query Editor:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="61209-3087">PSTN 總分鐘數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3087">PSTN Total Minutes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3088">持續</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3088">Minutes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3089">總分鐘數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3089">Total minutes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3090">所選時間範圍內的總分鐘使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3090">Total minute usage in the selected time range.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-3091">PSTN 入站總分鐘數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3091">PSTN Inbound Total Minutes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3092">持續</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3092">Minutes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3093">所選時間範圍內的進貨分鐘總使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3093">Total inbound minute usage in the selected time range.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-3094">PSTN 輸出總分鐘數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3094">PSTN Outbound Total Minutes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3095">持續</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3095">Minutes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3096">所選時間範圍內的總輸出分鐘使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3096">Total outbound minute usage in the selected time range.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-3097">PSTN 作用中使用者計數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3097">PSTN Active User Count</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3098">使用者數量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3098">Number of users</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3099">在該日期期間，至少進行一個連接通話的使用者數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3099">The number of users who made at least one connected call during that day.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-3100">PSTN 平均通話持續時間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3100">PSTN Average Call Duration</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3101">持續</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3101">Minutes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3102">所選時間範圍內所有已連接通話的平均持續時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3102">The average duration of all connected calls in the selected time range.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-3103">通常，1:1 PSTN 呼叫是四到五分鐘。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3103">Normally, a 1:1 PSTN call is four to five minutes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-3104">不過，這個平均值可能會因每個公司而有所不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3104">However, this average can differ for each company.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-3105">PSTN 總入站併發通話計數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3105">PSTN Total Inbound Concurrent Call Count</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3106">通話次數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3106">Number of calls</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3107">一分鐘內同時進行中的活動輸入通話數量上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3107">Maximum number of simultaneous active inbound calls in a minute.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="61209-3111">P50 延遲</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3111">P50 Latency</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3112">時間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3112">Milliseconds</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3113">50% 的要求應比所給的延遲更快。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3113">50% of the requests should be faster than given latency.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-3114">P50 抖動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3114">P50 Jitter</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3115">時間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3115">Milliseconds</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3116">50% 的要求速度應該比指定的抖動更快。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3116">50% of the requests should be faster than given Jitter.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-3117">P50 資料包遺失率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3117">P50 Packet Loss Rate</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3118">百分</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3118">Percentage</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3119">50% 的要求應低於指定的資料包遺失率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3119">50% of the requests should have lower than the given Packet Loss Rate.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-3120">PSTN 外寄撥號延遲</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3120">PSTN Outgoing Post Dial Delay</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="61209-3121">時間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3121">Milliseconds</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3122">撥出通話所發生的延遲，從撥打號碼到來電者或呼叫方聽到響鈴的那一段時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3122">The delay that occurs on outgoing calls measured from the time a number has been dialed until the caller or called party hears ringing.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-3123">PSTN 內送出站撥號延遲</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3123">PSTN Incoming Post Dial Delay</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3124">時間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3124">Milliseconds</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3125">在撥出電話撥打電話給來電者或呼叫方聽到響鈴的時間之前所進行的時間或延遲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3125">The time or delay that occurs on incoming calls measured from the time a number has been dialed until the caller or called party hears ringing.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="61209-3126">PSTN NER 良好的百分比</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3126">PSTN NER Good Percentage</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3127">百分</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3127">Percentage</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="61209-3128">NER 會測量傳送給收件者的電話撥打電話數，以衡量網路的傳送呼叫能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3128">The NER measures the ability of a network to deliver calls by measuring the number of calls sent versus the number of calls delivered to a recipient.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="61209-3129">NER = （接聽電話 + 使用者忙碌 + 撥打沒有應答 + 終端拒絕 Seizures）/總嘗試撥打 x 100</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3129">NER = (Answered calls + User Busy + Ring no Answer + Terminal Reject Seizures）/ Total Attempt Calls x 100</span></span>|
||||

## <a name="filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="61209-3130">濾鏡</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3130">Filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="61209-3131">許多維度與測量值也可以用來做為篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3131">Many Dimension and Measurement values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="61209-3132">您可以在查詢中使用篩選來消除資訊，就像選取要在查詢中新增或加入資訊的維度或測量一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="61209-3132">You can use filters in your query to eliminate information in the same way you'd select a Dimension or Measurement to add or include information in the query.</span></span>
